    <script type="text/javascript">
        $(function () {
            $(".blur-results tr:nth-child(n+7) td").each(function (index) {
                var text = $(this).text();
                var lowercaseLettersConverted = text.replace(/[a-z]/g, "x");
                var uppercaseLettersConverted = lowercaseLettersConverted.replace(/[A-Z]/g, "X");
                var allConverted = uppercaseLettersConverted.replace(/\d/g, "2");
                if (allConverted.length > 0) {
                    $(this).html(allConverted.substring(0, 35));
                }
            });
        });
    </script>
